Real Situation of Disaster Relief in Hubei Province

Labor Relief Has Not Achieved Great Results

Agricultural Relief Begins to Be Implemented

Thousands of People Frozen to Death in Yangxin

A dispatch from Hankou states that this year's drought in Hubei Province is extraordinarily severe. The disaster area covers more than 90 million mu (Chinese acres), and the number of victims exceeds ten million. The phenomena of fleeing, suicide, looting grain, and robbery are heard everywhere. Because the government has established a Disaster Relief and Famine Prevention Committee and decided on engineering plans, 20 counties, including Wuchang, Echeng, Puji, Huanggang, Huangpi, Guangji, Huangmei, Yunmeng, Xiaogan, Yingcheng, Hanyang, Xianning, Jiayu, Huang'an, Macheng, Xishui, Qichun, Yangxin, Daye, and Jingshan, have given priority to setting up labor relief stations to implement labor-for-relief. Since the implementation, nearly three months have passed, and the suffering of the victims should have been slightly relieved. However, there are those who are burdened by receiving relief, which is a strange reversal of cause and effect. According to those who have come from the fields, this year's drought is severe, and people have no way to stay put. Before the government issued relief, the old and weak had already filled the ditches, and the strong had fled in all directions. When the labor relief personnel arrived in the counties, nine out of ten houses were empty. In order to complete the task, the labor relief personnel had to order the district and baojia chiefs to make a list of names and assign tasks such as digging ponds. Because many of the able-bodied men had fled, the district and baojia chiefs falsely filled out the rosters. By the time the work began, many could not report. Thus, people were arrested everywhere to do the work, as if they were capturing criminals. The people mistakenly believed that the government was conscripting labor, not providing relief, and fled again and again. In the end, the policy of benefiting the people turned into disturbing the people, which was completely beyond the government's expectations. As for opening granaries, this has also been implemented in many places. However, after the granaries were opened, most of the grain was moldy, probably due to the variety or moisture. Those who borrowed the grain could only weep. In addition, wealthy gentry in various places voluntarily opened their wallets to provide porridge, but there was little porridge for many people, causing them to fight with each other. The elderly, weak, women, and children still could not eat. Such things are too numerous to mention. In terms of agricultural relief, only more than 50,000 yuan has been allocated so far. Afterwards, the Rural Cooperative Committee, the Four Provinces Farmers Bank, the Rural Finance Relief Office of the General Headquarters, and the China International Famine Relief Commission will be entrusted to jointly handle the matter. It is still difficult to predict the results. Moreover, the government's price stabilization has achieved considerable results. It has now decided to open porridge kitchens to provide relief to the destitute. Li Huiwu, the administrative inspector of the second district and the magistrate of Yangxin County, recently telegraphed the province, stating that in only the sixth and seventh districts of the county, the number of victims who have frozen and starved to death has reached thousands. If one county is like this, others can be known. The main points of Li's telegram are recorded as follows: "The subordinate county has suffered from bandit disasters, followed by drought disasters. Houses are in ruins, and fields are scorched. The suffering of the people is difficult to express in writing. The sixth and seventh districts, which are adjacent to Wuru, have only recently been recovered. The strong have been slaughtered and coerced by bandits. The remaining people are either old, weak, or disabled. They cannot work to make a living, nor can they move far away to beg for food. They are trapped by hunger and cold, sitting and waiting to die. In recent months, the number of people who have starved and frozen to death in these two districts has reached more than a thousand. Such a tragic situation breaks the hearts of those who hear it and makes the eyes of those who see it water. In the blink of an eye, the end of the year is approaching and the weather is cold. If a way to provide relief is not urgently sought, I fear that countless victims will become the bones of starvation and freezing. I have previously requested approval to set up a refugee shelter in the county seat, but due to limited funds, there are not many people who can be accommodated, and the funds have been almost exhausted since August. I am worried and cannot sleep at night. I only implore your seat to bestow merciful clouds and allocate a large amount of relief funds so that it can continue to be managed." The current situation of the people in the disaster area can be seen from this. (5th)

International Commercial Telegram

—Reuters Special Commercial News Telegram, November 6—

New York and Chicago Markets Closed for Elections

November 6th is Election Day in the United States. All markets in New York and Chicago are closed. The following are the market prices for Canadian goods:

Gold and Silver

London Gold Price: The London gold price today is 139 shillings, 5 and a half pence, down one pence from yesterday.

London Silver Bar: The London silver market was uneventful this morning. The market was stable at the close. The spot price is 23 pence, 4375, and the future price is 23 pence, 5625. Speculators bought in, and China bought and sold.

Bombay Silver Bar: The Bombay silver market was stable today. The spot closing price is 64 rupees, 7 annas, up four pounds from yesterday.

Exchange Rates

British-American: The London foreign exchange market was quiet this morning. The British-American exchange rate remained stable. The opening price was 4 dollars, 9 cents, 9 and 3125, higher than yesterday's closing price of the British-American exchange rate by 3125. After the opening, the U.S. dollar strengthened slightly, and the exchange rate fell. The final price was 4 dollars, 9 cents, 8 and 125, lower than the opening price by one cent and 1875. Also, one U.S. dollar is equivalent to 4 shillings and 0180 British gold.

British-French: The opening price was 75 francs, 84, up six pounds. It immediately returned to 75 francs, 78. The British pound fell. At 2:00 p.m., the exchange rate was 75 francs, 65, lower than the opening price by 19 pounds.

Cotton and Wheat

Indian Cotton: The Bombay cotton market was stable today due to purchases by European exporters. At 5:30 p.m., the price of white Locke cotton for April and May was 209 rupees, the same as yesterday.

British Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market soared today. At 1:00 p.m., the price for January was 6.65, up 18 pounds.

British Wheat: The Liverpool wheat market rose sharply today, with the increase being greater than yesterday's decline. At 1:00 p.m., the price for December was 5 shillings, 1 pence and 25, up one pence and 25.

Rubber: The London rubber market was looser this morning. At noon, the transaction price for January to March was 6 pence, 375, down 0625.

After the Remnants of the Jiangxi Bandits Crossed the Gan River and Fled Westward

The Main Force of the Bandits Seems No Longer in Jiangxi

Many Bandits Killed and Wounded in Xinfeng and Nankang

A dispatch from Nanchang states that the Red bandits in southern Jiangxi and western Fujian are collapsing step by step. Last month, the pseudo-Central Military Conference resolved to abandon the old nest and allow scattered bandits to lie dormant on the east bank of the Gan River and the Jiangxi-Fujian border to contain the National Army. Another large force was gathered to try to cross the Gan River and flee westward with all its strength. Before fleeing, they also feigned an attack on the front line of the Southern Route Army to create a smokescreen. In reality, the remnants of the pseudo-First Army Corps of Lin Biao, the pseudo-Third Army Corps of Peng Dehuai, the pseudo-Fifth Army Corps of Dong Zhentang, and the pseudo-Eighth Army Corps of Zhou Kun completely broke through Xinfeng and Nankang, and fled westward through Chongyi, Shangyou, and Suichuan. According to a recently announced message, after the bandits broke through Xinfeng, they set up pontoon bridges at Longhui, Jixian, and Nvbu, where Xinfeng, Nankang, and Dayu meet, and occupied Nankang. One group entered Chongyi from Qinglongxu, between Nankang and Dayu, and another group entered Chongyi from Yangmeisi, where Nankang and Chongyi meet. This is the left route of the bandits. The right route went from Zhongtangken and Dalongbu in Ganzhou to Suichuan and Shangyou. According to news from Ganzhou, more than 10,000 bandits who fled from Longhui on the 28th of last month entered the seventh district of Gan County. The purpose is unclear. It is confirmed that there are no bandit traces in Nankang County, but the pigs raised by the people in the places where the bandits passed have been slaughtered and eaten without leaving any. The bandits who crossed the river westward through Daxiao Wo in Xinfeng via Yangmeisi and between Chongyi and You kidnapped several good people from Li Zanliang's house in Wugong Township. The bandits who fled from Xiong Yu towards western Hunan were thwarted in Wujing and fled back again, fleeing westward through the area north of here. According to a responsible person in the military, Ganzhou's city defenses are solid. At the moment, the National Army's north, south, and west routes have been linked together. The bandits can be surrounded and annihilated in the Wanan, Suichuan, Chongyi, and Shangyou areas. The bandits in the Nanxin Yu area have been bombed into pieces. The bandits travel by night and hide during the day, carrying branches and straw on their hats, extremely panicked and embarrassed. (November 5)

Shandong Province Promotes American Cotton

Excellent Results This Year

Experience in Promotion in Qidong

A dispatch from Jinan states that Qidong in Shandong Province is a cotton-producing area. This year, the Department of Construction promoted the improved cotton variety No. 36, established cotton industry marketing cooperatives, and the cotton industry has become increasingly developed. More and more farmers are planting cotton. The soil for planting cotton is best suited to sandy loam. The soil along the Yellow River in Shandong is mostly sandy loam, which is quite similar to the lower reaches of the Mississippi and Negro rivers, which are famous cotton-producing areas in the United States. Therefore, it is also suitable for planting cotton, especially in Qidong. Unfortunately, over the years, old varieties and old methods have been used for cotton planting, and improvements have not been made. The quality of cotton has declined day by day. In 1922, American Kim's cotton seeds were transported to Shandong and scattered among the people. Cotton farmers called it local foreign cotton. In 1927, the Second Cotton Experiment Station was established in Qidong. Yang Shaoyun served as the director, and together with technician Hu Changzhun, they jointly researched and cultivated improved cotton varieties. In 1928, Yang Shaoyun died, and Hu Changzhun continued his work, collecting various cotton varieties and repeatedly experimenting with cultivation. By 1932, they had cultivated the improved Jiang cotton variety No. 36, which had the best quality. Initially, seeds were propagated at this station. In 1933, 4,000 catties of seeds were obtained. A portion was distributed to the Zouping Rural Construction Research Institute, and a portion was distributed to cotton farmers in Qidong for trial planting. It is estimated that 400,000 catties of improved cotton seeds can be obtained, which is enough for the whole county to plant cotton this year. When the new cotton went on the market, most of the cotton produced was purchased by ginning merchants. The cotton field only received 70,000 to 80,000 catties of seeds, which was not enough for the cotton farmers in this county. Therefore, No. 40 and No. 47, which had been cultivated, and No. 36-2, which had been bred, were used to supplement it. A total of 200,000 catties were sown this year. In order to prevent the loss of cotton seeds, the Department of Construction organized the American Cotton Marketing Cooperative in Qidong and was responsible for technical guidance, planning marketing methods, and providing loans to help the economy of cotton farmers. At the same time, China Cotton Historical Records established a large-scale ginning factory in Qidong. The cotton produced by the cooperative members was all collected at the ginning factory. The ginning factory ginned out the seeds and then sold them to the cotton factory to avoid the loss or confusion of the seeds. Since February of this year, Chen Shican, a technician from the Department of Construction, went to Qidong to start organizing the cooperative. The organization was completed in April, with a total of 153 societies, more than 4,800 members, and 33,000 mu of cotton fields. After the establishment of the cooperative, the government was only in a guiding position, teaching new technologies and assisting in marketing. The internal affairs and regulations of the society were determined by the members. The most important thing was that the seeds could not be changed without the consent of the society. Loans and sales were handled by the cooperative as a whole. Members could not sell to a certain factory or borrow from a certain party alone. The intention of the Department of Construction in handling the cooperative was not only to provide help and preserve seeds in terms of technology, marketing, and economy, but also to have a deeper meaning. Various foreign businesses have considerable organizations, and all administrative management and improvement and promotion are easy to handle. Our country has never had such an organization, and management is not easy. Therefore, organizing cooperatives makes it easy to start all promotion plans. This year's situation with American cotton, because it was initially dry and then rainy, cotton was greatly affected, and the harvest only accounted for 70% of previous years. Not only China is like this, but the whole world is like this. However, the output is already quite considerable, with the highest yield per mu reaching more than 300 catties, and averaging 200 catties, 7 million catties of cotton can be harvested. The Qidong ginning factory is currently purchasing at a price of 12 yuan and 7 jiao per 100 catties, which is worth about 900,000 yuan. It cannot be said that it is small to produce 900,000 yuan of cotton in one year, and the rural economy can also be adjusted. The income per mu is about 25 yuan or more, which is 8 yuan or more higher than planting grain. This year, there are 33,000 mu of cotton fields, which is an increase of 15,000 mu compared to last year. This 15,000 mu of land has increased revenue by 120,000 yuan compared to last year. The original 18,000 mu of land planted with cotton was changed to improved cotton varieties this year, and the revenue per mu increased by 3 yuan, for a total increase of 54,000 yuan. According to statistics, new and old cotton farmers can increase their revenue by 170,000 to 180,000 yuan this year. It is estimated that more people will plant cotton in the coming year, and the output will increase. The cotton seeds produced this year are estimated to be 500,000 catties of No. 36, 700,000 catties of No. 47, 40,000 catties of No. 36-2, and 50,000 catties of No. 40, for a total of 1.29 million catties. The provincial government has allocated a special fund of 32,000 yuan to purchase this cotton seed, which can purchase 160,000 catties at 2 fen per catty, preparing to promote it to the 12 counties designated as cooperative promotion areas next year. Qidong County will specialize in No. 36 alone, while the others will be distributed to the eleven counties of Zhangqiu, Qingcheng, Gaoyuan, Boxing, Putai, Bin County, Huimin, Gaotang, Xiajin, Linqing, and Qiuxian. This year, drought and flood are uneven, resulting in a 30% reduction in harvest, which is a rare phenomenon. Next year, the same number will be calculated. This 1.3 million catties of improved cotton seeds can yield 56 million catties of cotton, and those that do not use improved varieties are not included in this number. Cotton is suitable for planting when there is water when sowing and growing, but it is taboo to rain after flowering. The climate in Shandong has more rain in April and May, but not in August and September, so it is very suitable for planting cotton. However, this year has changed, with very dry conditions in April and May, and a lot of rain in September, so cotton was greatly affected, and the time for harvesting cotton was delayed by one month. Therefore, it is best to irrigate cotton by diverting water, not relying on rain from the sky. It can be controlled by humans. The success of siphon irrigation will be used in the cotton industry in the future and will have a great effect. Moreover, during the green gauze tent period, bandits rise up, and public security is most affected. In the future, there will be more cotton planters and fewer high-grain planters. Public security in cotton-producing areas can be easily maintained, which is also a secondary benefit of the cotton industry.

Northwest Inspection Notes

— Special Correspondent for This Newspaper, Geng Ya

Petroleum and Coal Outside Jiayuguan

Jiuquan's mineral products include gold, coal, and asbestos (shaped like silk, elastic, white or greyish-green, soft as cotton, woven into cloth that cannot be burned, called "fire-resistant cloth"). However, gold mines and asbestos are no longer being continuously mined. The coal reserves are very large. Due to the need for fuel, locals still arbitrarily excavate it. The production areas are located on the northern slopes of the Qilian Mountains: Dahonggou, Xiaohonggou, Donggouliang, Dahuangou, and the Binggou area. Among them, the coal from Dahuangou is of the best quality. The other places like Dahonggou and Xiaohonggou emit a foul odor when burned due to excessive sulfur content. The daily output from all locations is approximately over two thousand catties. In the winter, when farmers are free, there are more people digging and the output also increases. At the production site, the price of coal is about 180 wen for every dou (approximately 35 catties), which is equivalent to 18 copper coins. Carried by ox carts and camels to the county seat, a journey of about 120 li (Dahuangou is 40 li further away), it only sells for 500-600 wen. If transportation were convenient, it could be transported and sold to other counties.

At 1 PM on the second day, we departed from Jiuquan. The west gate was not open, so we exited through the north gate and turned northwest. We soon crossed the Taolai River. The river water was flooding and the grassland was marshy, making travel difficult. Once we ascended the dry sand, although the bumps were severe, the road was quite straight. Looking out over the nearby suburbs, "Haibaibai" grass grew everywhere. The shape of its leaves resembles that of a cypress tree, and its texture is as succulent as amaranth, rich in salty taste, making it a top-quality forage. To the left, the snow-capped mountains, reliant on the heavens, were like jade tablets, glistening and sparkling in the sun, truly a spectacular sight. Before long, the carriage arrived at Jiayuguan, having traveled sixty li. It is located one thousand five hundred and twenty li southeast of Lanzhou, backed by the Black Mountain of Jiayu to the north, and relying on the Red Mountain of Qilian to the south. The fortress city is located in the middle, with its perilous nature formed naturally. However, there are few residents. Although the Sino-Russian treaty once opened the south port, the commercial center remains in Jiuquan. Furthermore, the fortress city is made of earthen construction, the border walls are collapsing, and there are paths through the mountains that could be used to attack the rear. Compared with Shanhaiguan, which relies on mountains and borders the sea, it is not as impressive. The inscription "The Mightiest Pass Under Heaven" seems excessive. Moreover, with the invention of modern firearms, warfare has advanced into three dimensions. Even if it were as grand as "The First Pass Under Heaven," if the defending soldiers are ineffective, the saying "geographical advantage is not as good as human harmony" still applies, and it would still be inevitably trampled by the iron hooves of imperialists. Passing through the pass, we entered a Gobi Desert, sloping downwards, covered with fine stones that appeared blue. Recalling the journey west from Lanzhou, Jiayuguan is almost a high point on a fish's spine, with the north and south mountain ranges converging and then spreading out again, greatly influencing the wind direction. There is a saying that "when it thunders at Jiayuguan, two meeting halls will fall in Hanzhong," which shows the variability and swiftness of the climate and wind force here.

Forty li west of the pass is Shuangjingbao, devoid of human habitation. It is said that there used to be many residents, all engaged in gold panning. Judging from the relics of the fortresses and courtyards, it seems likely. After another forty li, we arrived at Huihuibao and stayed overnight. This day's journey is commonly said to be one hundred and sixty li, but in reality, it is only thirty-seven kilometers, approximately equivalent to one hundred and ten li. The fort belongs to Yumen County and has over thirty households, mostly from the interior. Although there are inns, there are no food shops. Human habitation becomes even scarcer further west. There are no places to get supplies along the way, so it is necessary to bring dry rations and travel according to the stations to avoid sleeping in the wilderness. Near the fort, the fields are irrigated by the Baiyang River, and the harvests of millet, wheat, and poppies are all good. The river water is clear and does not freeze in winter. Ancient willows tower at the edge, and wild grasses sway. Land is reclaimed from the wilderness, and people cultivate it themselves, making it a small oasis outside the pass.

We departed the next morning (the third). We first passed through the Black Stone Gobi, undulating like waves, with many fissures and traps, commonly called "Nine Gullies and Eighteen Slopes, Three Steps Up and Two Steps Slide," which is quite a realistic description. Then, we saw two or three places with lush water and grass, very suitable for nomadic grazing. After about sixty li, we reached Chijinhu, which used to be a post station, but now it is just ruins and crumbling walls. Eighteen li later, we reached Chijinpu, with five or six households. There was a fork in the road outside the fort, but when we asked people, they all avoided answering. Suddenly, a postal runner arrived, and we learned that going left leads to Chijinbao, and going right leads to the main road to Yumen. After traveling a few more li, we passed a small soft sandy beach. To the left, we saw dense village trees and a lush green field, which is the old site of Yumen from the Tang Dynasty, now known as Chijinbao.

Ninety li southeast of Chijinbao, on the northern slopes of the Qilian Mountains, there is a river that abounds in petroleum, naturally seeping out onto the ground. During the reign of Emperor Tongzhi of the Qing Dynasty, villagers entered the mountains to mine gold and passed by it, leading to its discovery. They tested it by lighting it on fire, and the flames blazed fiercely, so they named the place Shiyouquan (Petroleum Spring) and the river Shiyouhe (Petroleum River). They have been digging pits and scooping it up ever since. The Dusi Camp of the fort extracts two thousand catties of oil as a donation each year. In 1928, the Dusi Camp was abolished, and the donation was collected by the Jiuquan city defense army. The oil area covers approximately ten square li. In winter and spring, heavy snow does not melt, and the oil also congeals and does not flow. In the summer, when the water rises, the oil begins to seep out. Villagers scoop up the oil and put it in buckets, carrying it ashore, and then oil merchants (currently there are three) transport it to various places in large carts to supply the villagers for lighting or to grease the axles of large carts. The sales are limited, which shows that the quality of the oil is not very good. In the early years of the Republic of China, a certain Belgian and a certain German brought it to Shanghai for analysis, and they believed that the composition was excellent. Later, they requested permission to develop it, but the provincial government did not approve it. In the spring of 1929, the Gansu provincial government sent an expert, Zhang Renjian, to investigate and brought it to Lanzhou for analysis. It was found to contain 16.50% gasoline and 70.00% kerosene. In addition, about forty li east of the Petroleum River, eighty li south of Huihuibao, and forty li south of Baiyanghe Village in the Shiyougou area, covering an area of six or seven li, also produces petroleum, and the composition is very similar to that of Petroleum Spring.

Gasoline is a volatile oil, the most valuable component of petroleum. Ordinary petroleum is considered to be a high-quality oilfield if it contains 10% or more gasoline. The use of gasoline is extremely important. Modern civilized countries all use gasoline as the primary power to drive machinery. Some even use the abundance of petroleum production and reserves as a standard for estimating the strength and wealth of a country. Taking the development of transportation in Northwest China as an example, airplanes and automobiles all require a large amount of gasoline. The gasoline used by the Eurasian Aviation and Ganxin Automobile companies, stored in Su (Jiuquan), is all imported goods from Tianjin and Shanghai, with each box costing about 70 yuan, seven or eight times more expensive than in Tianjin and Shanghai. However, this only takes into account transportation costs, and the huge losses of about a quarter due to prolonged shaking, breakage, and evaporation during transportation are not yet included. To abandon oneself and seek others, to let the rights and interests flow out, and to discard goods on the ground, is it not painful? Now, the development of the Northwest has progressed from theory to reality, and the oil mining in Shaanxi has also achieved remarkable results. It seems difficult to allow this great source of wealth to be abandoned again.

Fifty li west of Petroleum Spring is Honggou, one hundred and twenty li north is Beiyao, and one hundred and fifty li south of Yumen County is Changma, all of which produce huge amounts of coal. Zhaobi Mountain, north of Changma, produces green copper ore, commonly known as malachite, which contains trace amounts of copper. If deep exploration and mining are carried out, a large amount of copper ore will surely be discovered. As for gold mines, they are abundant everywhere along the northern slopes of the southern mountains, whether they have been panned or not.

Songjiang

Prohibition Committee Reviews and Approves Opium Sales and Smoking Establishments

The County Opium Prohibition Committee has repeatedly issued orders to various districts, urging them to register opium smokers nearby in order to issue opium smoking licenses. As the deadline for obtaining licenses has passed, there are still a few who are waiting and watching, which hinders the prohibition policy. Therefore, the Committee has ordered the Public Security Bureau to conduct a thorough investigation. Anyone who smokes opium without a license, regardless of whether they have registered or not, should be severely punished in accordance with Articles 2 and 6 of the Regulations on Opium Smoking Licenses in Various Counties. Furthermore, there have been as many as 150 to 160 applications for registration to open opium sales and smoking establishments in this county. The Prohibition Committee, based on the proportion of opium smokers who have obtained licenses, reviewed them in conjunction with the four section chiefs and decided to approve the establishment of 37 establishments in the first district, 15 in the second district, 9 in the third district, 8 in the fourth district, 15 in the fifth district, 8 in the sixth district, 16 in the seventh district, and 4 in the eighth district. The Committee has issued a notice limiting those who are approved to pay the fees and fill out the forms within seven days in order to forward them to the provincial capital for the issuance of licenses.

County Government Holds Baojia Training Session

The county government recently decided to organize Baojia, based on Article 5 of the Schedule of Progress for Organizing Baojia in the Provincial Compilation of Laws and Regulations. It assembled district chiefs and assistant district chiefs as members of the organizing committee to hold training sessions, scheduled to be held on the mornings of the 8th, 9th, and 10th of this month, starting at 9:00 AM, and in the afternoons, starting at 2:00 PM, in the county government conference room. The training will cover the responsibilities of the district chiefs, the investigation of households, the significance of organizing Baojia, and the procedures for implementation. County Magistrate Jin has issued separate orders for compliance. It is reported that the county government has also selected and appointed Baojia organizing committee members for the eight districts in this county: Fei Fusheng in the first district, Qin Zhonghe in the second district, Zheng Junshan in the third district, Shen Shoutian in the fourth district, Wu Changding in the fifth district, Zhu Haoru in the sixth district, Shen Jusan in the seventh district, and Li Zengxin in the eighth district.

Taicang

Extension of契税 Reduction for Another Three Months

The deed tax (契税) in this county was originally levied at 9% for sales and 6% for mortgages. From May of this year, it was reduced to 6% for sales and 3% for mortgages for a limited period of three months. Later, the deadline was extended for another three months, expiring at the end of October. It should have been terminated and the tax rate restored to 9% for sales and 6% for mortgages. However, this summer, there was a severe drought, and the autumn harvest was poor, causing economic hardship for the people. Due to previously established contracts, they were unable to pay the tax within the deadline. It has now been decided to extend the reduction of 6% for sales and 3% for mortgages for another three months, from November 1st of this year to January 31st of next year. For sales deeds, the total amount of tax and surcharges levied per hundred yuan of deed value is 8.3 yuan of silver, including 6 yuan of silver for the regular tax, 0.667 yuan of silver for the Zhongzi donation, 0.667 yuan of silver for the property donation, 0.666 yuan of silver for the construction donation, and 0.3 yuan of silver for the collection fee. For mortgage deeds, the total amount of tax and surcharges levied per hundred yuan of deed value is 3.9 yuan of silver, including 3 yuan of silver for the regular tax, 0.5 yuan of silver for the Zhongzi donation, 0.25 yuan of silver for the construction donation, and 0.15 yuan of silver for the collection fee.

Launch of Combined Ship and Train Tickets

The Jing-Hu (Beijing-Shanghai) and Hang (Hangzhou) Railway Administration had previously signed a contract for third and fourth-class combined tickets with the Louqin Shipping Bureau in this county. Recently, due to the poor performance of the shipping line, the Railway Administration terminated the contract and signed a contract with Qingyang Renji Shipping instead, with procedures scheduled to take effect on December 1st. The one-way fare from Taicang to Shanghai is 5.5 jiao (角) for fourth-class and 8.5 jiao for third-class. The shipping line runs from Qidun through Qingyang Port Station, Taicang, Shuangfeng, Zhitang, and Shaxi.

Suzhou

All District Chiefs of the County Resign

The district chiefs of the autonomous districts in Wu County, due to being ordered to implement Baojia and having their expenses reduced by two-thirds, are experiencing great difficulties in their work. Five district chiefs, including Wu Erchang of the first district and Wang Shande of the second district, have successively submitted their resignations. County Magistrate Wu has retained them. Now, the district chiefs feel that there is really no solution to the financial problems, so they are determined to resign en masse. They have appointed Wu Erchang to draft the resignation letter, which they will all sign and submit to the county government tomorrow (the 8th). County Magistrate Wu has submitted this matter to the provincial office for instructions.

Wu County Implements Regional Joint Defense

County Magistrate Wu Qiyun of Wu County, in view of the recent repeated incidents of theft in various villages, causing unrest among the rural population, and with the imminent arrival of winter, deemed it urgent to prepare for winter defense to maintain security. Therefore, on the afternoon of the 5th, he convened the heads of the water and land police forces to hold a winter defense meeting. County Magistrate Wu chaired the meeting and reported the purpose of the meeting. It was decided to establish the Wu County Winter Defense Committee, and nine people, including Colonel Zhu of the Military Police Regiment, Colonel Ma of the Engineering Regiment, District Chief Zhou of the Second Water Police District, County Magistrate Wu, and Chief Wang of the Public Security Bureau, were appointed as standing committee members. November 15th was set as the start date for the winter defense, and the winter defense period was tentatively set for four months. The entire county was divided into five major security zones, with a winter defense office established in each zone.

Baoshan

Repeated Disputes within the Party, Public Organizations Request Serious Handling

The Baoshan County Party Headquarters, due to repeated disputes, was ordered to cease operations in the summer of this year. The Jiangsu Provincial Party Headquarters appointed Wang Bingyi as the custodian, and the matter came to a temporary end. It is now heard that the provincial authorities plan to restore Baoshan Party affairs and will appoint Zhu Xuedian and others as organizing committee members. Upon hearing this, the Baoshan County Education Association, the County Farmers' Association, and other public organizations believed that Zhu's daily behavior was improper and that he had been dismissed by the authorities for corruption in handling civil education affairs. If he were to be appointed to organize Baoshan Party affairs, it would inevitably lead to renewed disputes. Therefore, they jointly telegraphed the Provincial Party Headquarters, requesting a serious handling of the matter. The party members in various districts of the county also jointly submitted a petition to the Jiangsu Provincial Party Headquarters, listing the causes and consequences of the repeated disputes in Baoshan Party affairs over the years, requesting that they be carefully considered to avoid further disputes.

Jiading

Police Station Chief and All Officers Taken into Custody

The firearms of the former Public Security Branch Bureau of Loutang Town were borrowed from the local area. After the branch bureau was reorganized into a police station, Patrol Chief Ye Rongchun transferred the loan receipt for continued use. In the middle of last month, a C96 pistol and a handgun, placed in the station, suddenly disappeared. Despite a thorough search, they could not be found. Patrol Chief Wu reported the situation to the County Public Security Bureau. Bureau Chief Chen Youmin ordered that the case be solved within a time limit. As the deadline passed without any progress, Bureau Chief Chen believed that the loss of firearms at the station was not due to any special circumstances and was obviously stolen by the internal police officers. The day before yesterday, he personally led seven police officers to the town and took Patrol Chief Ye and fourteen police officers of the station back to the bureau for detailed interrogation. He also transferred Chief Gao of the bureau and six police officers to temporarily take over the station.

Wuxi

Jiang Minsheng Comes to Wuxi to Give a Speech

Jiang Minsheng, a major general in the Northeast Volunteer Army who resists Japan, is originally from Wen County, Shandong Province, and is currently 39 years old. He has recently been touring various places to give speeches. He arrived in Wuxi from Suzhou the day before yesterday to contact the County Party Headquarters, the Education Bureau, and others to arrange speeches and distribute printed propaganda materials. The content is alarming and moving, and he is vigorously promoting domestic goods. It is reported that Jiang plans to stay in Wuxi for a week and then go to Beijing, Anhui, Jiangxi, Hunan, Sichuan, Hubei, Fujian, Guangdong, Guangxi, and other places to give speeches.

新民报 Reporter Suffers Abuse, Fellow Journalists Hold a General Membership Meeting to Provide Assistance

Pan Yuyi, a reporter for the Xinminbao newspaper in this county, was accused of fraud for paying a fine on behalf of someone. He was arrested and detained by Zhang Yu, the director of the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau, and Fan Shouchi, an officer of the bureau. He was sent to the headquarters and transferred to the court for questioning. However, when Pan was detained at the detention center of the First Branch, Director Zhang stripped him of his outer clothing and forced him to endure the cold all night. When Pan was escorted to the headquarters by the bureau, Zhang again ordered the chief police officer to tie him tightly with hemp rope and drive him through the streets. Upon hearing this, all the members of the Journalist Association of this county believed that since Pan's alleged crime had been transferred to the judiciary, they could quietly await the handling of the case according to the law. Moreover, the alleged fraud was not comparable to major cases of murder and theft. They unanimously expressed their indignation at Zhang Yu's abuse of power. At the same time, based on Pan Yuyi's report of being illegally abused, they requested assistance. The association held a general membership meeting at the Railway Hotel at 4:00 PM yesterday. More than twenty members attended, including Shi Jilin, Chen Hongjun, Sun Chunpu, Zhang Xiongliang, Sun Xiangfeng, Zhang Suichu, and Xu Xiyin. Sun Dexian chaired the meeting. The following matters were resolved: (1) Ratification of the decision of the Standing Committee to suspend Pan Yuyi's membership; (2) Sending a letter of inquiry to Zhang Yu; (3) Submitting petitions to the county government and the Public Security Bureau to remove Zhang Yu from office and investigate his case; (4) Engaging three lawyers, Sun Zuhong, Zhou Beiwu, and Tang Ying, to jointly study the legal issues involved in this case.

Changshu

Gunfight with Bandits at Nanzhang Bridge

At around 12:00 AM on the 3rd, three bandit boats suddenly arrived in Nanzhangjia Bridge, a village belonging to the Third District. The boats, which had come from Huadang, carried approximately 20 to 30 bandits, all armed with long guns. After reaching the town, they disembarked, intending to loot the entire town. Three or four bandits first guarded the north and south ends of the town. Fortunately, the sentry of the Liantang Security Corps noticed the bandits disembarking. Seeing the crowd, they ran to the Corps headquarters to report, and an emergency assembly was immediately called. However, the bandits seemed to have noticed, and they immediately opened fire to resist arrest. The Corps soldiers then hid in the fields and returned fire. The two sides exchanged fire for thirty minutes. The residents of the area, hearing the dense gunfire, knew something was amiss and got up to sound the gongs. The bandits, realizing that they were outnumbered, boarded their boats and fled back towards Huadang. In the end, there were no casualties on either side, but an elderly woman surnamed Bu in the village was hit by a bullet and seriously injured. She has now been sent to Wuxi for treatment.

Jiangyin

Embezzlement Case in the County's Field Tax Office

The county government's Field Tax Office has previously experienced embezzlement through internal and external collusion. Chen Ruizhang, the former director of the Field Tax Office, resigned due to opium addiction. Chen Jingxin replaced him as acting director. Regarding the embezzlement, County Magistrate Bao convened representatives from various agencies to discuss and appointed auditors to investigate. After more than a month of investigation, a portion of the grain records were audited, and embezzlement amounting to over 3,000 yuan was discovered. The unaudited portion is likely to be even greater. Yesterday (the 5th) at around 5:00 PM, County Magistrate Bao, believing that the employees of the record room had embezzled state taxes, immediately ordered Zhang Rui, the captain of the First Company of the Security Corps, to detain He Jishi, Zhao Zhen, Jiang Jiuyu, Zhai Guangying, and Zhai Baozi, five employees of the internal record room and the external record room. At around 9:00 PM, Gu Wenhua, the chief of the Second Section, interrogated them. Two employees of the external record room, Zhai Yongkang and Zhai Shaopeng, had already fled upon hearing the news. The county ordered the police to summon Wang Yu, the owner of Jubao, the owner of De Tang Xi Hao, and Wang Xunyuan, the owner of Tai He Tang, to the station, ordering them to hand over Zhai Yongkang and others within a time limit. The case is now expanding significantly. The county government must also report it to the Department of Finance and appoint a commissioner to thoroughly investigate it to clear up the accumulated malpractices in the field tax system.

Bandits Loot Villages in Shangdang

Earlier this month, at approximately 10:00 PM, more than ten bandits broke into the home of Luo, a resident of Shangdang Qingjiang Taiwan. Each was armed with long and short guns. Two of them, holding short guns, pointed the gun barrels at Luo's wife and daughter-in-law and ordered them not to make any noise or they would be killed. At that moment, the two women were frightened and did not dare to make a sound, allowing the bandits to search for about an hour. The bandits took all the valuable belongings in the house, worth several thousand yuan, and fled.

Qingjiang

News of the Construction of the Huaiyin Ship Lock Project

The淮委會 (Huai River Commission) is constructing a ship lock at Yangjiazhuang South Zhong Matou in Huaiyin, concerning the project to connect the 裏运水 (Li Canal) with the water of the river. Construction began this spring. The riverbed is 15 meters deep, and the distance between the banks is about 100 meters. The canal extends from Yangzhuang in the north to the 裏运 (Li Canal) in the south, with a total length of more than one里 (Chinese mile). Currently, in addition to a portion of the workers transporting stone and materials, more than 100 are taking care of the machinery and driving piles, engaging in the repairing and construction of the lock foundation. Each pile is more than two丈 (Chinese feet) long and about three尺 (Chinese feet) thick. There are six pile-driving machines working day and night. Engineer Wang Yizeng and Deputy Engineer Yin Chengsan are permanently stationed at the construction site to supervise the progress. According to them, if the lock foundation project continues to work day and night at the current pace, it will be completed soon. In any case, the lock project will be completed before the flood season next year.

Two Kidnapping Cases Outside the City, Noted

On the evening of the second day, six or seven bandits suddenly came to Yadian Lane outside Huaiyin City, Hebei, and kidnapped Xu Hongjun, the manager of the Wansheng Pig Farm in the lane, and Xu Yongqing, who was in charge of the disaster relief station. At the same time, in Hongfuzhuang, a village outside the dike, bandits came to the home of Hu Kaiyu, a villager, each carrying long and short guns. They forbade Hu's family from making a sound. Then, they searched all the rooms and found Hu Kaiyu's sixteen-year-old son and Hu Kaiyu's nephew, who was only ten years old. The bandits grabbed both children and left with shouts. After the incident, although numerous security police inside and outside the dike pursued them, they did not know where the bandits had gone.

Hongyu Cloth Shop Suddenly Liquidates

Due to the impact of the economic downturn in recent years, closures of large and small stores have been frequently heard in Hangzhou. Last month, Kaitai Cloth Shop suddenly announced liquidation, owing depositors approximately 370,000 yuan. Creditors have been negotiating with the manager of the shop, Li Jintang, to repay the debts, but no solution has been reached. Unexpectedly, Hongyu Cloth Shop in Qinghefang also announced liquidation yesterday. The shop has been in business for 60 years, with annual sales of approximately 700,000 to 800,000 yuan. In recent years, sales have decreased to approximately 200,000 yuan, resulting in significant losses. Manager Liu Zixing entrusted a lawyer to announce liquidation. It is reported that the amount owed is 250,000 yuan, including approximately 200,000 yuan to silver shops. There are not many depositors. Currently, there are approximately 60,000 yuan in goods and 70,000 yuan in accounts receivable, which are insufficient to repay the debt of approximately 120,000 yuan. After receiving the report, the city government sent personnel to join the City Chamber of Commerce to thoroughly investigate the business accounts and ordered the shop manager to submit a detailed explanation of the reasons for the liquidation.

Borrowing Boxer Indemnity Funds to Develop Jiang-Zhe Fisheries

Later, the Ministry of Railways joined the collaboration, and the project expenses were shared equally by the ministry and the province, so funding was secured. Therefore, the loan of 130,000 pounds sterling, equivalent to more than 2,100,000 Chinese dollars, has been decided to be jointly borrowed by Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces for the development of fisheries in the two provinces. The Boxer Indemnity Committee has approved it. It is planned to use the funds to purchase a large number of fishing vessels and new-style fishing gear from London, England, for the development of fisheries.

More Than Thirty Homes Burned Down in Hongxing Bridge

It took one hour for the fire to gradually subside. A total of more than thirty households were burned down, along with more than fifty shi (石，a unit of dry volume) of rice.

Page 9

Local News

### Details of the "Jiahe" Steamer Robbery in Shantou Waters

Pirates' Goal Was a Large Sum of Money

Frustrated, They Kidnapped Crew Members

One Maritime Policeman Killed, One Wounded

The "Jiahe" steamer, a Shanghai-Xiamen-Shantou liner of the state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, was robbed by pirates in Shantou waters on the 4th of this month while sailing from Shantou back to Shanghai. One maritime policeman was shot and killed, and one was wounded. Three people, including the business director, were kidnapped before the pirates left. Yesterday's report briefly mentioned the telegram. Further details are as follows:

Transporting Funds to Xiamen

The Xiamen branch of the Shanghai China Industrial Bank also has banknotes in circulation. In order to replenish its cash reserves, the bank negotiated with the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company on October 29th to transport 300,000 silver dollars to Xiamen. Each box contained 5,000 silver dollars, totaling 60 boxes. They were loaded onto the ship at the Jinliyuan Wharf. The most numerous other goods were soybean cakes, about 10,000 several thousand pieces, followed by wheat flour, about six or seven thousand bags, and the rest were textiles, cigarettes, and other items. The company, considering the large amount of money on board, did not take on passengers, hence the journey from Shanghai to Xiamen was very safe. On the 2nd of this month, the ship arrived in Xiamen, and the money was unloaded and the cargo and passengers were cleared. Then, the ship set off for Shantou.

Pirates' Misunderstanding

After the "Jiahe" arrived in Shantou, it loaded passengers and cargo on the 4th and set sail north to Shanghai. However, the Dapeng Bay pirates have informants stationed at important ports throughout the country, who specialize in gathering information about ships' itineraries and whether they carry valuables, in order to commit robberies. This time, the "Jiahe" transported funds from Shanghai to Xiamen. The pirates mistakenly believed that the funds were being transported from Shantou to Xiamen or Shanghai. Therefore, twelve pirates disguised themselves as passengers on the 4th and infiltrated the ship, waiting for an opportunity to rob it. It is known that the "Jiahe" is already 41 years old and is not a regular passenger ship, so it was not equipped with iron grilles. Only six escort team members were assigned, each given weapons, to protect the ship.

Robbery in Shantou Waters

At 7:00 AM on the 4th, the "Jiahe" set sail from Shantou. There were only a few dozen third-class passengers on board. At 9:15 AM, the ship arrived at the Tai Sarni Point in the Dashanmian Cape waters, only 50 li away from Shantou. The pirates on board started the robbery. The head bandit fired a shot as a signal, and the other eleven pirates responded simultaneously. First, they put the captain, Sha Zengjia, and the radio operator, Chen Guoxiong, under surveillance. Then, they drove the first and second officers and other crew members into a room and forced the captain to change direction and sail towards Haifeng. At this time, the entire ship was under the control of the pirates. The crew had lost their ability to resist and had no choice but to obey them.

Maritime Policeman Killed

The maritime police on board heard the gunshots and knew it was a robbery. They immediately plotted resistance. However, the pirates had paid attention to this when they boarded the ship, so they struck first. Before the maritime police could draw their guns, the pirates opened fire. One maritime policeman was shot and killed on the spot, falling to the ship's deck. Another maritime policeman was also wounded by the pirates. The other maritime police did not dare to move again and were disarmed. Even the self-defense weapons in the captain's room were taken away.

Search and Robbery

The pirates' goal was the 300,000 silver dollars. Therefore, when they robbed the ship, they first detained the business director, Shen Qinxiang, and the treasury official, Li Shaobing, and ordered them to hand over the money. Shen and others handed over the cash stored in the treasury, but had no other large sums of money to hand over. The pirates still did not believe them and ordered them to hand over the keys to the cargo hold and open the cargo hold. After the pirates searched carefully and confirmed that there was no large amount of cash, they realized that the 300,000 silver dollars transported from Shanghai had already been unloaded in Xiamen. The pirates then expressed their disappointment. According to statistics, the pirates' search and robbery on the ship lasted from 9:00 AM on the 4th to 6:00 AM on the 5th, a total of 22 hours.

Kidnapping of Crew Members

On the morning of the 5th, the ship, under the control of the pirates, sailed towards Honghai Bay, east of Haifeng. Along the way, the pirates seized a fishing boat to use for their escape. When they reached Honghai Bay, the pirates disembarked onto the fishing boat and left. Before leaving, because they had robbed so little, they kidnapped the ship's business director, Shen Qinxiang, the treasury official, Li Shaobing, and another cargo clerk. After the pirates left the ship, the captain, Sha Zengjia, released the detained people, repaired the engine, and withdrew from Honghai Bay, sailing towards Xiamen.

Report to Shanghai

The ship's wireless radio had been damaged by the pirates, so the authorities could not be notified immediately when the pirates left. It was not until 7:00 AM yesterday morning that the Shanghai office received a telegram from Sha Zengjia, which briefly stated: "Our ship set sail from Shantou at 7:00 AM on the 4th. At about 9:00 AM, when the ship arrived at Shantou, it was robbed by twelve pirates. One member of the ship's escort team was shot and killed by the pirates, and one was wounded. The pirates forced our ship to sail to Honghai Bay, east of Haifeng. Before leaving, they kidnapped one business director and two cargo clerks. The ship is now sailing towards Xiamen." The telegram was very brief and did not mention the amount of losses.

Families Inquire

After reading the newspaper and learning about this incident, the families of the crew members in Shanghai rushed to the headquarters yesterday morning around 10:00 AM to inquire about the truth. The most anxious were the families of the business director, Shen Qinxiang, the treasury official, Li Shaobing, and the cargo clerk, who all wanted to ask about the names of those who were kidnapped. However, the company only knew the names of Shen and Li and did not know the details. They had to comfort them with kind words and promise to investigate by telegram. Only then did they disperse.

Request to Apprehend Pirates

After receiving the report, Liu Hongsheng sent a telegram to Zhu, the Minister of Transportation of the Nanjing government, yesterday, requesting him to forward it to the Ministry of the Navy, and to telegraph the authorities of Fujian and Guangdong provinces, requesting them to send troops and police to cooperate in the arrest of the pirates and rescue the three kidnapped crew members. The company also directly telegraphed the Xiamen Naval Command and the Guangdong Navy, requesting them to send warships to intercept the pirates, in the hopes of capturing them. At the same time, they telegraphed Xiamen, ordering the "Jiahe" to return to Shanghai as soon as possible. Yesterday, it was heard that the British destroyer HMS "Visham" had sailed to Shantou and Honghai Bay to assist in the pursuit of the pirates.

Arrival Tomorrow

After the pirates left, the "Jiahe" first went to Shantou, sent a telegram to Shanghai, and then left Shantou for Xiamen. The ship's wireless radio is currently being repaired by Chen Guoxiong along the way. Yesterday afternoon, the Shanghai office received a telegraph from Xiamen, stating that the "Jiahe" had safely arrived in Xiamen. After loading some goods, it immediately set sail back to Shanghai. It is expected that the ship will arrive safely in Shanghai at 3:00 PM on the 8th. All losses will only be known after the ship arrives. As for the maritime police who were killed and wounded by the pirates, the deceased will be properly buried after the ship arrives in Xiamen, and the wounded will be sent to a hospital in Xiamen for treatment. It is heard that the company will provide them with considerable compensation.

Hu Wenhu Visited the City Center Yesterday Morning

The Two Railways Host a Special Train to Visit the Mausoleum on the Anniversary of Sun Yat-sen's Birth

November 10th to 13th

The Two Railways Administration is taking advantage of the anniversary of Sun Yat-sen's birth to promote travel. It is scheduled to hold a mausoleum visit tour from November 10th to 13th. During this period, all stations that sell round-trip excursion tickets to the Nanjing Railway Station can sell round-trip excursion tickets. Each station can also sell group fare reduction tickets according to regulations. If the number of people is too large, they must send a letter to the Traffic Department in advance to arrange a special train to facilitate the mausoleum visit. The section chief of the Jingdan section of the Traffic Department will be responsible for providing reception services on a daily basis during the prescribed period. The travel arrangements are as follows: (1) All cities along the Two Railways line from Zhabei to Nanjing can participate. (2) Those who wish to participate in the mausoleum visit will receive the following benefits: A. Fares: Individuals or small groups of less than 20 people can purchase round-trip excursion tickets from the stations that sell round-trip excursion tickets (first and second class tickets are 75% of the regular price, second-class tickets are 85% of the regular price). Groups of 20 or more people can purchase group tickets. B. Train Numbers: If you wish to reserve seats on a certain train, add carriages to a certain train, or reserve a special train on a certain day, you can discuss it with the stationmaster or business office on the spot. The railway will give priority and preferential treatment. C. Tour Guides: If participants need a special tour guide, they can indicate it on the registration form in advance for proper preparation. D. Accommodation: If passengers need to book hotels and arrange accommodation, they can state it in advance, and we will do our best to arrange it within our capabilities. (3) All passengers on the Two Railways visiting the mausoleum will be given a special mausoleum visit publication, with a tour itinerary of the capital and exquisite landscape illustrations as souvenirs. (4) Those who wish to arrange a special mausoleum visit train must register in advance, no later than 5:00 PM on November 6th. The date and time of the special train and the special stops will be announced two days before departure (i.e., November 8th) according to the temporarily determined results.

Mao Yisheng Talks About the Start Date of the Qiantang River Railway Bridge

The groundbreaking ceremony is scheduled for the 11th of this month in Hangzhou

The total construction cost is set at 4 million yuan

The Ministry of Railways and the Zhejiang Construction Department will cooperate to complete it in a year and a half

The Ministry of Railways and the Zhejiang Construction Department are preparing to build the Qiantang River Railway Bridge. It has now been decided that the groundbreaking ceremony will be held in Hangzhou on the 11th of this month, and work is actively underway. In terms of funding, the Ministry of Railways and the Zhejiang Construction Department will each bear 2 million yuan, for a total of 4 million yuan. The project is expected to be completed in about a year and a half. At that time, east-west traffic in Zhejiang will be connected, and the railways will be connected and operated together, which will greatly benefit the development of industry and commerce. Our reporter interviewed Mao Yisheng, the director of the Qiantang River Bridge Engineering Office, last night. The details of his conversation are as follows:

Groundbreaking Ceremony Scheduled for the 11th

According to Mao, the groundbreaking ceremony for the Qiantang River Railway Bridge has been set for the morning of the 11th of this month in Hangzhou. Invitations will be sent to people from all walks of life in Beijing and Shanghai to attend. The invitation cards will be co-signed by the Ministry of Railways and the Zhejiang Construction Department. It is hoped that the Shanghai press will send personnel to Hangzhou to participate.

Total Cost of 4 Million Yuan

As for the total cost of the project, the initial funding included 1 million yuan from the National Economic Commission, 2 million yuan borrowed by the Shanghai Banking Group, and £160,000 allocated by the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Fund. However, now that the Ministry of Railways and the Zhejiang Construction Department have decided to cooperate, it has been decided that each will bear half of the total cost, that is, the Ministry of Railways will raise 2 million yuan from the Sino-British Bank and the Construction Bank, and the Zhejiang Construction Department will still borrow 2 million yuan from the Shanghai Banking Group, for a total of 4 million yuan. The Ministry of Railways has appointed Counselor Xia Guangyu as its representative, and the Zhejiang Construction Department will be represented by Director-General Zeng Yangfu.

Budget Exceeded, Joint Planning

The initial budget for the entire project was indeed 5 million yuan, but now, after bidding, it has been proven that it will not exceed 4 million yuan. In the future, if the bridge is completed and the tracks are connected at both ends, if the funds are insufficient, both parties will be responsible for planning.

Bridge Foundation Engineering is Solid and Permanent

The bridge foundation engineering is divided into two parts. On the Zhabei side, the six piers are constructed using caisson method. On the Xixing side, the nine piers are constructed using piling method, with a length of 100 feet driven in. The entire bridge has sixteen spans, each with a distance of 220 feet. The entire project is expected to be completed in about a year and a half. The engineering will strive for solidity and durability, and will definitely not last only three or five decades. Mao concluded by saying that the office will have a formal written report with details of the project, and hopes that it can be disclosed in the newspapers before the groundbreaking ceremony on the 11th.

The International Trade Bureau Introduces Domestically Produced Products

Tung Oil, Silk Cocoons, and Woolen Fabrics

Manufacturers can contact the Bureau

Germany Needs Our Tung Oil

According to the International Trade Bureau, tung oil is a special product of China, and the provinces of Sichuan, Guizhou, Hunan, and Hubei have the largest output. In recent years, remote areas in Zhejiang, Anhui, and Shanxi have also gradually planted and manufactured oil. Chinese tung oil has always been praised by paint manufacturers in Europe and America. Tung oil has the characteristic of drying quickly and can be used as a raw material for paint. To date, there are no other vegetable oils that can replace it, so exports have increased year by year, and it has a significant position in international trade. The Czech Biedma Industrial Company and the German Mr. Dossig have written to request tung oil. It is hoped that all tung oil exporters will notify the Bureau so that they can be introduced.

Czech Republic Willing to Manage Our Silk Cocoons

Also, Adam & Co. of the Czech Republic has written to express its willingness to manage and promote Chinese silk cocoons and woolen fabrics. Manufacturers who wish to promote their products to that country are requested to notify the Trade Bureau at No. 1040, Beitu, New Garbage Bridge.

"Wuyang" Steamer Has Been Rescued

Stranded Until the Night of the 3rd

The "Wuyang" steamer, which was stranded outside Dashigang, was heavily loaded and deeply drafted, and its hull was deeply mired in the shallows. The shipowner repeatedly tried to reverse the engine, but failed to escape the danger. After three days and three nights, it was towed out by a ship sent by the Guangzhou branch of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company when the tide rose. Fortunately, the area was a sandy beach and there were no stones or reefs, so although the ship was stranded for a long time, the bottom of the hull was not greatly damaged. Yesterday, a telegram was sent to Shanghai saying that it could load cargo and leave Guangzhou for Shanghai immediately.

Municipal Bonds Have Been Printed

Exchange Will Begin from Yesterday

Entrusted to the Bank of China

The 3.5 million yuan of Shanghai Municipal Bonds issued in 1934 were underwritten by the American Anderson & Co. After public subscription, they were sold out. Now that the bond certificates have been printed, Anderson & Co. has entrusted the Bank of China to exchange them. The bank issued a special announcement yesterday, stating that the municipal bonds have now been printed. Those who hold temporary receipts from the bank are requested to exchange them for formal bonds at the bank's trust department starting from the 6th of this month. This is a special announcement.

The Jiaxu All-Zhejiang Drought Relief Association held a regular meeting yesterday and decided to order rice and flour for relief. The details are as follows:

Meeting Situation

Xu Qianlin, Hu Fengxiang, Zheng Yuzhou, Qian Xinzhi, Xu Jilun, Chu Huiseng, Zhang Shenzhi, Qian Junren, Yu Zhongxian, Gu Qixian, Yu Zuoting, Lu Zhinan, Wang Xiaolai, Zhang Xiaolin, Du Yuesheng, Qu Wenliu, Zha Zhongjian, Kui Yanfang, Shen Tianxin, Xu Yongzuo, He Dekui and other 20 people attended.
