Shen Bao Local Supplement - Automobile Weekly

Notes on 1935 American New Cars

— Dun Ne

Not many changes in style and mechanism

Two major goals: economy and comfort

Time passes so quickly. The year 1935 is already upon us. Not to mention anything else, just in terms of changes in car styles, many new cars are launched on the market at the end of the year and the beginning of the year. Customers get rid of the old and welcome the new, and they can't help but be busy again. Although it is only late autumn weather now, the engineers of European and American car factories are racking their brains to plan for next year's new cars. Some car factories have not only completed their plans, but even announced their prototype cars. However, most of the American manufacturers are currently in a state of intense activity. According to a report from Detroit, the center of American automobile manufacturing, at the end of last month, there is a general description of the changes in various cars for the coming year. The general idea is that 1935 cars will not have significant changes in style and mechanism. The price will be as low as possible in order to promote car sales and expand the market.

American-made cars are roughly divided into three categories in terms of price. One type is expensive cars, with high prices. One type is mid-priced cars, which are slightly cheaper than high-priced cars. There is also the most common type of low-priced cars, which are specially supplied to the general public. Because these three types of cars have different prices, the styles and mechanisms are inevitably different. It is said that among the new cars of 1935, the mid-priced and high-priced cars will not have much change compared to the current 1934 models. It seems that they want to extend the life of the 1934 cars for another year. The reason for this is to maintain the current selling price and not increase it, so that the future of the automobile industry can improve.

It is not difficult to make more reforms and improvements to a car. However, these changes, such as changes in style and improvements in power, all require extra money. In the end, this money will inevitably be added to the customers. If business is booming and purchases are strong, even if the car price increases a little, it can still be sold. However, if the goods are not selling well and the sales are sluggish, then difficulties will arise. If you want to promote sales, customers will hesitate to buy because of the price, so the factory has to reduce the selling price in order to get rid of the stock. Such increases and decreases in price are actually very troublesome. Not only that, but sometimes it will also lose the customers' trust, as if going back on your word and the factory is indecisive, causing disappointment to the buyers. Therefore, the American mid-priced and high-priced car factories, in order to avoid the various troubles of increasing prices due to changes in style and mechanism and repeating the original price due to sluggish sales, simply take a wait-and-see approach for a year. For the new cars of 1935, they take a conservative and prudent attitude, and do not hope for obvious innovations in order to compete for short-term gains.

Speaking of low-priced cars, the situation is somewhat different. The competition between factories is very fierce. It can be said that each factory shows its ingenuity and unique ideas. Therefore, how the new cars of next year will change is still difficult to say for the time being. However, significant changes are indeed inevitable. There are three large factories in the United States that produce low-priced cars. These three are almost household names and do not need to be introduced. They are now "building cars behind closed doors". In the late winter and early spring, they will "show their faces" to everyone. At that time, there will inevitably be a lot of excitement. Now, according to the plan, the engineers and experts of these cars claim that most of the design work is almost ready. However, their work is still very busy and it seems that it will not be completed until the end of the year. Therefore, people generally speculate that these new cars will probably meet everyone at the end of this year. When the new year arrives and everything is revived, these cars with the largest sales and the best value will inevitably be active again.

The number of car sales is also very related to time. There are several periods of the year when car sales are very good, and there are also several periods when they are somewhat inferior. Taking this year as an example, three quarters have already passed, and only winter remains. The most prosperous time for car sales is in the early summer months of January and February. After late autumn, the peak of sales has passed and it gradually declines. The closer it gets to the time when new cars are about to be launched, the more sluggish the sales of various cars become. The reason for this is that customers who buy cars at this time are unwilling to buy a new car rashly. They must wait until the grand automobile exhibition is over before deciding on their choice. Therefore, in the months of October and November, the period of seasonal decline has arrived. Car dealers cannot have very extravagant hopes. It is estimated that the total number of American cars produced this year will be around 2,800,000.

Ford's production plan is almost independent of other companies. Therefore, the design and manufacture of new cars can be improved as much as possible. It is said that the new model of its 1935 car will be seen by the public in November of this year. The new model of the Packard truck has already appeared a month ago. Studebaker was even earlier than Packard. It has already shown its appearance to the public this summer. There are also many of them circulating on the market now. The new products of other manufacturers will probably not be able to show their colors until January 1st next year.

The suspension of the National Automobile Exhibition gives the manufacturers great freedom. Because in previous years, as the meeting date approached, everyone inevitably worked day and night in order to produce new cars in time. Now that the opening has been delayed, there is plenty of time to plan everything. The biggest feature of the 1935 new cars and the biggest goal of everyone's research and reform is economy, safety and comfort. As for speed and power, the current various cars are already very capable of dealing with them.

According to an automobile manufacturer, "Automobile manufacturers are very clear that if the automobile business is to prosper, the only way to do it is to start with not increasing the selling price. Therefore, the reason why this year's manufacturers are not prepared to make strong changes is to lower the selling price. If a car is to be changed to a new model, the selling price will increase a lot as a result." After hearing these words, we can understand why each car factory is not prepared to make significant changes to the new cars. On the other hand, we can also speculate that the general economic recovery is not as satisfactory as expected.

Among the three most popular low-priced cars on the market, the competition between two of the car companies is fierce, and the reform is also diligent. Almost every time a new car is launched on the market, there are always some new tricks to offer to the public. They will never be unknown in the past. Therefore, Ford Motor Company is constantly improving its new products. One of them is said to be born in November of this year. Everyone believes that this new car is generally very light and slightly streamlined in form.

Chevrolet has been planning its new car for six months. Speaking of the style of its car body, it seems to be almost like a semi-streamlined LaSalle. As for the new Chevrolet's engine, whether it will continue to have six cylinders or adopt eight light cylinders is still undecided. Therefore, outsiders have no way to speculate. Both straight-six and V-eight engines have been manufactured and tested in the Chevrolet factory.

Next year's Plymouth new car will be larger in style. The motor used has been greatly changed, so the power has also increased a lot. As for the streamlining of the appearance, it is always a little worse than its United Branch products, the DeSoto and Chrysler. The Walter P. Chrysler is said to have major changes in style. The reforms of other cars are probably not many. The accessories of next year's new cars will also be improved in order to increase sales. The shortcomings of the 1934 cars that have been discovered over the past year will be remedied. In short, the biggest goal is to strive for a beautiful style with a little streamlining.

Overview of the Hillman New Car

— Fu

Taking "Safety First"

As the principle of construction

Recently, people in the automotive industry often tell each other that the British automotive construction skills and mechanical engineering genius can be seen from the various styles of the newly released Hillman cars. I have tasted the general public. Therefore, there are many notable features of Hillman's theory. Therefore, even if we occasionally take a look, we will know its quality. Excellent and outstanding, it is not comparable to ordinary similar products. According to the past twelve months, the factory has not made any major innovations for Hillman's new cars. However, its various improvements have greatly contributed to comfort and modern driving pleasure. As far as the current car situation in the city is concerned. Then this kind of progress is not very shallow.

The new car is currently on display in the sample room of Fulin Automobile Company on Daxilu Road. The machinery is sophisticated and the construction is ingenious. It is indeed a masterpiece of British products. All the manufacturing, no matter the size, is based on "safety first". It is an unbreakable principle. The all-steel frame is equipped with an all-steel body. They complement each other and are extremely strong. In addition, the automatic spring organization used for the car body device can be automatically calibrated to the appropriate degree regardless of the load. Therefore, the road surface is trembling and tilting. The troubles are completely eliminated invisibly. The person who is in the car feels like sitting on an easy chair. It feels very comfortable and comfortable. As for the arrangement, even beginners can easily handle it. Because the gears it is equipped with are harmonic. The new ventilation system is another important feature of the Hillman new car. Whether it is cold or summer, it can be adjusted at will. Enjoy the extreme refreshment without feeling any discomfort from the wind or stuffiness. This is especially commendable. It is the Hillman's unique lining device. This was invented several years ago. Today it has become a standard feature of Hillman. And because it has been improved many times. More perfect. Therefore, the so-called lining force device. The greatness of its effect is unmatched by all other shock absorbers. It has been generally recognized. There is no doubt. The front and rear seats of the Hillman are very spacious. The various styles produced are extremely spacious and comfortable. This is because of the re-arrangement of the pads, footrests, etc. It is extremely ingenious.

Hubei Construction Department Organizes Truck Gasoline Consumption Measurement Experiment

— Fu

According to Hankou communications, the Hubei Provincial Construction County has actively promoted construction in the province. Highways have been completed one after another. The number of trucks used has increased sharply. Therefore, gasoline has become a major daily expense. In order to save money and avoid false consumption. In order to do so, a collection of various freight cars used on each road was made. On Wednesday of last week, each vehicle's local sales company drove the car to a place about ten miles away from Huangpi. To measure the gasoline consumption of each vehicle.

This measurement was presided over by the Jian Department. The organization is strict. The handling is serious. Therefore, the result is very reliable. Every freight car participating in the measurement. Before the start of the measurement, a specified weight carefully weighed. Loaded on it. By the time the gasoline in the gasoline tank is cleared. And the engine is driven. After the last drop of car fuel is exhausted by the carburetor. Then each with five gallons of gasoline. Store in the oil pool. Officially set off. During the race, a special car from the Jian Department led the way. Always maintain its speed at 30 miles per hour. The vehicles participating in the competition. Then follow closely behind. Line up. There is a considerable distance between each car. And another special car hall behind it. As for the supply car, it is far away at a certain distance. And arrived at Huangdian Village. Stop for food. And after taking pictures. Then return. So it should be like all cars. The gasoline is exhausted. The engine suddenly stopped. If you don't add fuel, you can't move forward. Then the special car of the Jian Department. Detailed inspection of the mileage traveled by each car. As a result, the Chevrolet truck performed best. A total of five gallons of gasoline. 67 miles of travel. The average fuel consumption per gallon is 13.4 miles.

A General Overview of the 1935 Auburn New Car

— Yun

Two Major Groups: Eight-Cylinder and Six-Cylinder

A Total of Eight Styles

The 1935 Auburn new car has now been released for use by people from all walks of life. The new cars are divided into two major groups, each with four styles, namely sedan, convertible sedan, brougham, and convertible sedan roadster. The Auburn eight-cylinder car has a wheelbase of 127 inches and 115 horsepower. The six-cylinder version has a wheelbase of 120 inches and 85 horsepower. Both groups of new cars emphasize streamlining, but there are no dramatic changes in their appearance. The design of the front and engine hood of the new cars is particularly exquisite and captivating. Auburn products were originally divided into standard and luxury groups, but the factory no longer uses this method for the 1935 models. This is because each style of the new car is fully equipped. The headlights and radiator grilles of the new cars are all chrome-plated, shining brightly and pleasing to the eye. All the conveniences for passengers are complete, allowing you to do whatever you want while in the car, with extreme ease. The car body is longer and lower, making the space more spacious. The front seats are particularly wide, now allowing three people to sit side by side, which is also extremely comfortable. The new low-pressure shock absorbers and air-cushioned rubber brackets eliminate or minimize the impact of all bumps. The dual-ratio rear axle reduces engine speed while the car continues to travel at high speed. This equipment can be installed on both groups of cars, but it requires additional payment. The latest ventilation system features divided windows on the front doors and movable windows on the rear doors. The engine uses lead cylinder heads, providing abundant power and enhanced performance. The valve operation and cooling system have made great progress. Notably, the power plants installed in both groups of new cars are extremely economical. All oil purifiers, air purifiers, mufflers, mechanical fuel pumps, and heat exchangers are fully equipped. The car body is made of pure steel

Page 22

, making it extremely safe. Even all noises are prevented from occurring. The driving panel is also made of steel and is an integral part of the car body. In short, every part of the new car has been carefully researched and designed, so it can be safely asserted that it will be welcomed everywhere.

Reduction in Car Accident Cases in the UK

— Gan

—An Average of Two Fewer Deaths Per Day—

Car accidents are a major problem in the UK that is difficult to solve. The government is sparing no effort to ensure safety in transportation. Recently, the Minister of Transport, Mr. Hore-Belisha, gave a public broadcast speech, stating that in the past three months, namely July, August, and September, the number of road accidents resulting in death has decreased compared to the past, even compared to the same period in 1933. According to the statistics available to Mr. Hore-Belisha at the time, the reduction reached 6.5%. In terms of numbers, there were approximately 140 fewer deaths.

However, according to on-the-spot inquiries, the numbers reported by Mr. Hore-Belisha are still below the actual numbers. In the three months of July, August, and September this year, the actual number of deaths caused by cars was 175 fewer than the same period last year, or 8%. Therefore, in terms of days, in this quarter, the number of deaths caused by car accidents in the UK has decreased by about two people per day. According to past experience, the three months of July, August, and September are usually the most dangerous period of the year, with a higher incidence of fatal accidents than at other times. Moreover, at the beginning of this year, there were more car accidents than in the same period last year, so the current results are particularly commendable.

According to the authorities, the reduction in car accident cases in the UK is due to the implementation of road safety policies and the public's attention to road safety issues promoted by the Ministry of Transport. The Minister of Transport often publishes the number of road accident cases to inform the public and constantly encourages people to pay attention to road safety. The figures are published per 100,000 people in each city, allowing for comparison. As a result, the authorities and the public in each city have to use the most effective methods to reduce the number of accidents, as the existence of such facts is a flaw for each city.

The Ministry of Transport publishes weekly reports on road accident cases occurring in the suburbs of London, using statistical methods to clarify the location, cause, and result of the tragedies. According to Mr. Hore-Belisha, this method is quite effective in solving this problem. However, it is unfair to compare towns without considering the size of their population or area. Nevertheless, the greatest benefit of this statistic is to promote the joint attention of the local police and the Ministry of Transport to the locations where accidents occur and to concentrate their efforts to solve and prevent them. If each location can benefit from this statistic and address it with genuine dedication, then a significant reduction in road accident cases is to be expected. In fact, the results of studying statistics often reveal that certain types of accidents frequently occur in certain locations or venues. Thus, the constant presence of danger can be addressed at any time. For example, the cause of the accident can be investigated, whether it is due to the improper laying of tram tracks, the dangers of road intersections, or dark corners of the road, and can be resolved one by one.

The Minister of Transport is also planning a method of implementation, intending to have local authorities learn methods of reducing road accident cases from maps. These maps have already been posted for use, clearly indicating where car accident cases are most likely to occur. The newly formed Road Safety Committee will also use these maps to achieve the most detailed statistical methods and their practical effectiveness. Some people involved in the automotive industry find the regulations set by the public to be annoying, but these regulations do contribute to the prosperity of the automotive industry. Some leaders in the automotive industry believe that the more car accidents are reduced, the more people will buy cars. Therefore, they often provide great assistance in promoting the implementation of measures to curb car accidents.
